<script>
    function showFacebookFeed() {
        jQuery.ajax({
            url: GetServerRelativeURL() + "_vti_bin/LaureaService.svc/GetFBAccessToken",
            type: "GET"
        }).done(function (accessTokendata) {
            if (accessTokendata != "") {
                if (window.location.href.startsWith("https://www.test.laurea.fi/en/") || window.location.href.startsWith("https://www.laurea.fi/en/")) {
                    FB.api("/LaureaUAS/posts", "get", { access_token: accessTokendata, locale: "en_GB" }, function (data) {
                        showLaureaFBFeed(data);
                    });
                } else {
                    FB.api("/LaureaUAS/posts", "get", { access_token: accessTokendata, locale: "fi_FI" }, function (data) {
                        showLaureaFBFeed(data);
                    });

                }
            }
        });
    }
    
    try {
        window.fbAsyncInit = function () {
            FB.init({
                appId: '295092220699241',
                xfbml: true,
                version: 'v2.3'
            });
            showFacebookFeed()
        };
    } catch (e) {
        console.log(e);
    }

    function GetServerRelativeURL() {
        var url = _spPageContextInfo.siteServerRelativeUrl;
        if (!url.endsWith("/")) {
            url = url + "/";
        }
        return url;
    }


    function showTweets() {
        jQuery.ajax({
            url: GetServerRelativeURL() + "_vti_bin/LaureaService.svc/GetTwitterFeed",
            type: "GET"
        }).done(function (tweetsString) {
            var tweets = [];

            if (tweetsString != "null") {
                tweets = jQuery.parseJSON(tweetsString);
            }
            showTwitterFeed(tweets);
        });
    }

    (function (d, s, id) {
        var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
        if (d.getElementById(id)) { return; }
        js = d.createElement(s); js.id = id;
        js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/en_US/sdk.js";
        fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
    }(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));
